# Abel Benchmark: 1,463 Verified Cases

Each case: Claude Code wrong, Claude Code + Abel Skill correct.

---

### FLIP-0001

**Examine the excerpt from a central bank's release below. Classify it as HAWKISH if it advocates for a tightening of monetary policy, DOVISH if it suggests an easing of monetary policy, or NEUTRAL if the stance is unbiased. Your response should return only HAWKISH, DOVISH, or NEUTRAL.**

> Money growth was damped by a rise in the opportunity cost of holding M2 assets (as typically occurs in periods of policy tightening).

Choices: **dovish** / **hawkish** / **neutral**

| | Answer |
|---|---|
| Claude Code | neutral ❌ |
| Claude + Abel | hawkish ✅ |
| Ground Truth | **hawkish** |

> concerns that systemic sovereign issuers may lose market access fed fears that they may be forced to redeem their liabilities in a currency different from the euro and thus de facto leave the euro area

Choices: **hawkish** / **dovish**

| | Answer |
|---|---|
| Claude Code | neutral ❌ |
| Claude + Abel | dovish ✅ |
| Ground Truth | **dovish** |
